                        adRefreshRateDeskSectionBucket = parseInt( strikeConfigDynamicProps.adRefreshRateDeskSectionBucket, 10) || 30,
                        adSizesDeskSectionBucket = strikeConfigDynamicProps.adSizesDeskSectionBucket || [],
                        adPrefetchMarginDeskSectionBucket = parseInt( strikeConfigDynamicProps.adPrefetchMarginDeskSectionBucket, 10) || 500;

                    window.foxstrike.cmd.push(function(Strike){
                        Strike.loadAd({
                            target: '#desktop_desk-hp-lb10',
                            iu: 'desk/hp/lb10',
                            sizes: (function(){
                                var adSizesDeskSectionBucket = strikeConfigDynamicProps.adSizesDeskSectionBucket || [],
                                    adSizes = adSizesDeskSectionBucket;
                                return (adSizes && adSizes.length > 0) ? (adSizes.split(',')) : [];
                            })(),
                            pos: 'desktop',
                            props: {
                                adRefreshRate: adRefreshRateDeskSectionBucket,
                                adPrefetchMargin: adPrefetchMarginDeskSectionBucket
                            }
                        });
                    });</script></div><section class="collection collection-section good-news" data-intcmp=""><header class="heading"><h3 class="title"><a href="//www.foxnews.com/category/good-news" data-omtr-intcmp="fn_hp_sb_good-news_buckettitle">Good News</a></h3><div class="more"><a href="//www.foxnews.com/category/good-news">View All</a></div></header><div class="content"><div class="latest"><article class="article"><div class="m"><a href="//www.foxnews.com/sports/super-bowl-lvii-merchandise-losing-team-will-still-serve-big-purpose" data-omtr-intcmp="fn_hp_sb_good-news_thumbnail1"><img src="//global.fncstatic.com/static/orion/img/clear.gif" data-src="//a57.foxnews.com/static.foxnews.com/foxnews.com/content/uploads/2023/02/480/270/rams-von-miller-super-bowl.jpg?tl=1&amp;ve=1" data-srcset="//a57.foxnews.com/static.foxnews.com/foxnews.com/content/uploads/2023/02/320/180/rams-von-miller-super-bowl.jpg?tl=1&amp;ve=1 320w,//a57.foxnews.com/static.foxnews.com/foxnews.com/content/uploads/2023/02/480/270/rams-von-miller-super-bowl.jpg?tl=1&amp;ve=1 480w,//a57.foxnews.com/static.foxnews.com/foxnews.com/content/uploads/2023/02/768/432/rams-von-miller-super-bowl.jpg?tl=1&amp;ve=1 768w" alt="Super Bowl LVII merchandise of losing team will still serve a big purpose"></a></div><div class="info"><header class="info-header"><div class="meta"><span class="eyebrow is-articles"><a href="https://www.foxnews.com/sports">Sports</a></span><span class="time" data-time-published="2023-02-11T21:55:09.000Z"></span></div><h2 class="title"><a href="//www.foxnews.com/sports/super-bowl-lvii-merchandise-losing-team-will-still-serve-big-purpose" data-omtr-intcmp="fn_hp_sb_good-news_articletitle1">Super Bowl LVII merchandise of losing team will still serve a big purpose</a></h2></header></div>
